Chest and Back, Abs and Calves

Power Training with Chest 
Bench Press: 20 reps first set, then 10, raise weight to go immediately to 5 reps, 3 reps and 1 rep. 
Continue with as many sets as possible (at least 5) for 1-2 reps
Perform last set with lighter weight that permits high repetitions 
Go to Incline Presses and do the same thing. Follow with DB Flys
